## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([Start]) --> ReadArgs[Read Command Line Arguments]
    ReadArgs --> InitSpark[Initialize SparkContext & SQLContext]
    InitSpark --> ReadBase[Read Base Parquet Data from S3]
    ReadBase --> FilterNull[Filter: final_stop_arrived_at NOT NULL]
    FilterNull --> FilterLoc[Filter: final_stop_location_id = destination_newloc_id]
    FilterLoc --> ReadOrgs[Read Organizations Parquet]
    ReadOrgs --> JoinOrgs[Join Base with Orgs on created_by_org_id]
    JoinOrgs --> FilterOcean[Filter: ship_mode_id = 5 Ocean]
    FilterOcean --> ReadStatus[Read Shipment Statuses Parquet]
    ReadStatus --> JoinStatus[Join with Shipment Statuses]
    JoinStatus --> FilterTime[Filter: status created before arrival]
    FilterTime --> CalcSeconds[Calculate shipment_status_to_arrival_seconds]
    CalcSeconds --> FilterPositive[Filter: seconds > 0]
    FilterPositive --> AddDayOfWeek[Add day_of_week Column]
    AddDayOfWeek --> ReadLoc[Read Location Data]
    ReadLoc --> JoinLoc[Join with Location for City/State]
    JoinLoc --> FilterWindow[Filter: Last 365 Days]
    FilterWindow --> FilterCodes[Filter: Specific Status Codes]
    FilterCodes --> AddSunThru[Add sun_thru_thurs Flag]
    AddSunThru --> SaveRaw[Save Raw Data to S3]
    SaveRaw --> ReadRaw[Reload Raw Data]
    ReadRaw --> LoopModels{For Each Model in MODEL_MAP}
    LoopModels --> CalcWindow[Calculate Window Statistics]
    CalcWindow --> CalcStdDev[Calculate stddev_distance]
    CalcStdDev --> FilterOutliers[Filter: -1.5 <= stddev_distance <= 1.5]
    FilterOutliers --> GroupBy[GroupBy Rollup Keys]
    GroupBy --> AggStats[Aggregate: 30/60/90/120/180/365 Day Stats]
    AggStats --> WriteRedis[Write to Redis via redis_bulk_load]
    WriteRedis --> WriteParquet[Write Parquet to S3 Versioned & Latest]
    WriteParquet --> NextModel{More Models?}
    NextModel -->|Yes| LoopModels
    NextModel -->|No| End([End])
```

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Main
    participant Spark
    participant S3
    participant Redis
    
    Main->>Spark: Initialize SparkContext

    Main->>S3: Read base.parquet

        Main->>Spark: Calculate Window Statistics

        Main->>Spark: GroupBy & Aggregate
        Main->>Redis: Bulk Load via redis_bulk_load
        Main->>S3: Write Latest Parquet
        Main->>S3: Write Versioned Parquet
    end
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
graph TD
    subgraph Models
        M1[shipment_ocean_latlng_city]
        M2[shipment_ocean_latlng_status_city]
        M3[shipment_ocean_latlng_status_city_dayofweek]
    end
    
    subgraph Rollup_Keys
        R1[lnglat_whole + city]
        R2[status_code + lnglat_whole + city]
        R3[sun_thru_thurs + status_code + lnglat_whole + city]
    end
    
    subgraph Aggregations
        A1[30_day_mean/std/count/percentile_60]
        A2[60_day_mean/std/count/percentile_60]
        A3[90_day_mean/std/count/percentile_60]
        A4[120_day_mean/std/count/percentile_60]
        A5[180_day_mean/std/count/percentile_60]
        A6[365_day_mean/std/count/percentile_60]
    end
    
    M1 --> R1
    M2 --> R2
    M3 --> R3
    
    R1 --> A1
    R1 --> A2
    R1 --> A3
    R1 --> A4
    R1 --> A5
    R1 --> A6
    
    R2 --> A1
    R2 --> A2
    R2 --> A3
    R2 --> A4
    R2 --> A5
    R2 --> A6
    
    R3 --> A1
    R3 --> A2
    R3 --> A3
    R3 --> A4
    R3 --> A5
    R3 --> A6
```

## Diagram 6

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> ReadData
    ReadData --> FilterData
    FilterData --> JoinOrgs
    JoinOrgs --> JoinStatus
    JoinStatus --> CalculateMetrics
    CalculateMetrics --> JoinLocation
    JoinLocation --> FilterDateRange
    FilterDateRange --> ProcessingLoop
    
    state ProcessingLoop {
        [*] --> SelectModel
        SelectModel --> CalcWindowStats
        CalcWindowStats --> FilterOutliers
        FilterOutliers --> AggregateStats
        AggregateStats --> WriteRedis
        WriteRedis --> WriteS3
        WriteS3 --> CheckMore
        CheckMore --> SelectModel: More Models
        CheckMore --> [*]: Done
    }
    
    ProcessingLoop --> [*]
```
